def predict(features, zone=None):
    # Main prediction function.
    # Zones: ['0', '1', '2', '3']
    if zone is None:
        zone = assign_zone(features)
    if zone == '0':
        return predict_zone__0(features)
    elif zone == '1':
        return predict_zone__1(features)
    elif zone == '2':
        return predict_zone__2(features)
    elif zone == '3':
        return predict_zone__3(features)
    return None
